    59‚Üí
    60‚Üí        // Create drink log for today
    61‚Üí        let drinkLog = DrinkLogEntity(
    62‚Üí            logDate: today,
    63‚Üí            startedAt: today,
    64‚Üí            drinkTypeId: DrinkTypePreset.beer.rawValue, // Beer: 5% alcohol
    65‚Üí            quantity: 350 // 350ml * 0.05 = 17.5g alcohol
    66‚Üí        )
    67‚Üí        try await serviceContainer.drinkLogRepository.save(drinkLog)
    68‚Üí
    69‚Üí        // Create sleep log for today
    70‚Üí        let sleepLog = SleepLogEntity(
    71‚Üí            logDate: today,
    72‚Üí            difficultyFallingAsleep: 2,
    73‚Üí            nightAwakening: 3,
    74‚Üí            earlyAwakening: 2,
    75‚Üí            unrefreshed: 3
    76‚Üí        )
    77‚Üí        try await serviceContainer.sleepLogRepository.save(sleepLog)
    78‚Üí
    79‚Üí        // Act
    80‚Üí        let trends = try await service.getDayWiseTrends(days: 1)
    81‚Üí
    82‚Üí        // Assert
    83‚Üí        let todayTrend = trends.first { $0.weekday == weekday }!
    84‚Üí        XCTAssertEqual(todayTrend.avgDrinkCount, 1.0)
    85‚Üí        XCTAssertEqual(todayTrend.avgAlcohol, 17.5, accuracy: 0.01)
    86‚Üí        XCTAssertEqual(todayTrend.drinkingRate, 1.0)
    87‚Üí        XCTAssertEqual(todayTrend.avgSleepScore, 2.5, accuracy: 0.01) // (2+3+2+3)/4 = 2.5
    88‚Üí    }

   182‚Üí    func testCorrelationStrengthFromValue() {
   183‚Üí        // Strong correlation
   184‚Üí        XCTAssertEqual(CorrelationStrength.from(0.8), .strong)
   185‚Üí        XCTAssertEqual(CorrelationStrength.from(-0.75), .strong)
   186‚Üí
   187‚Üí        // Moderate correlation
   188‚Üí        XCTAssertEqual(CorrelationStrength.from(0.5), .moderate)
   189‚Üí        XCTAssertEqual(CorrelationStrength.from(-0.45), .moderate)
   190‚Üí
   191‚Üí        // Weak correlation
   192‚Üí        XCTAssertEqual(CorrelationStrength.from(0.3), .weak)
   193‚Üí        XCTAssertEqual(CorrelationStrength.from(-0.25), .weak)
   194‚Üí
   195‚Üí        // No correlation
   196‚Üí        XCTAssertEqual(CorrelationStrength.from(0.1), .none)
   197‚Üí        XCTAssertEqual(CorrelationStrength.from(0.0), .none)
   198‚Üí    }

     4‚Üí@MainActor
     5‚Üífinal class SwiftDataUserPreferencesRepository: UserPreferencesRepositoryProtocol {
     6‚Üí    private let modelContext: ModelContext
     7‚Üí    private let defaultId = \"default\"
     8‚Üí
     9‚Üí    init(modelContext: ModelContext) {
    10‚Üí        self.modelContext = modelContext
    11‚Üí    }
    12‚Üí
    13‚Üí    func get() async throws -> UserPreferencesEntity {
    14‚Üí        let id = defaultId
    15‚Üí        let predicate = #Predicate<UserPreferencesEntity> { entity in
    16‚Üí            entity.id == id
    17‚Üí        }
    18‚Üí
    19‚Üí        var descriptor = FetchDescriptor<UserPreferencesEntity>(predicate: predicate)
    20‚Üí        descriptor.fetchLimit = 1
    21‚Üí
    22‚Üí        if let existing = try modelContext.fetch(descriptor).first {
    23‚Üí            return existing
    24‚Üí        }
    25‚Üí
    26‚Üí        // Create default preferences
    27‚Üí        let defaults = UserPreferencesEntity()
    28‚Üí        modelContext.insert(defaults)
    29‚Üí        try modelContext.save()
    30‚Üí        return defaults
    31‚Üí    }
    32‚Üí
    33‚Üí    func save(_ entity: UserPreferencesEntity) async throws {
    34‚Üí        modelContext.insert(entity)
    35‚Üí        try modelContext.save()
    36‚Üí    }
    37‚Üí
    38‚Üí    func update(_ updateClosure: (UserPreferencesEntity) -> Void) async throws -> UserPreferencesEntity {
    39‚Üí        let preferences = try await get()
    40‚Üí        updateClosure(preferences)
    41‚Üí        preferences.update()
    42‚Üí        try modelContext.save()
    43‚Üí        return preferences
    44‚Üí    }

    48‚Üí        let id = defaultId
    49‚Üí        let predicate = #Predicate<UserPreferencesEntity> { entity in
    50‚Üí            entity.id == id
    51‚Üí        }
    52‚Üí
    53‚Üí        let descriptor = FetchDescriptor<UserPreferencesEntity>(predicate: predicate)
    54‚Üí        let existing = try modelContext.fetch(descriptor)
    55‚Üí        for entity in existing {
    56‚Üí            modelContext.delete(entity)
    57‚Üí        }
    58‚Üí
    59‚Üí        // Create new defaults
    60‚Üí        let defaults = UserPreferencesEntity()

### Current State Classification

**Mixed Language Approach (Problematic)**:
- The app has **intentional Japanese UI** (Settings, Trend Analysis screens)
- But many screens use **English** (Dashboard, Drink Log, Sleep Log, Morning Condition)
- **No systematic localization mechanism** - languages are hardcoded directly into code
- This is an inefficient, non-scalable approach that makes it difficult to:
  - Support additional languages
  - Maintain consistency
  - Update strings without code changes
  - Localize user-facing error messages"

## Implementation Plan: iOS Localization for YoakeMae

### Recommended Approach: String Catalogs (`.xcstrings`)

For iOS 17+, **String Catalogs** (`.xcstrings` format) is the recommended approach over traditional `.strings` files. Here is why:

**Advantages of String Catalogs:**
1. **Single file management** - One `.xcstrings` file contains all languages in JSON format
2. **Automatic string extraction** - Xcode automatically detects localizable strings from SwiftUI
3. **Built-in editor** - Xcode provides a visual editor with translation status tracking
4. **Better merge conflict handling** - JSON format is more git-friendly than binary `.strings` files
5. **Native SwiftUI integration** - Works seamlessly with `Text()`, `LocalizedStringKey`, and `String(localized:)`
6. **iOS 17+ is the minimum target** - This project already targets iOS 17.0

---

### File Structure for Localization Resources

```
ios/YoakeMae/
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Resources/
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Info.plist
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Assets.xcassets
‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Localizable.xcstrings        # NEW: Main string catalog
```

The String Catalog will contain translations organized by:
- **Source language**: Japanese (ja) - since Japanese is the primary language
- **Target language**: English (en)

---

### project.yml Changes Required

```yaml
name: YoakeMae
options:
  bundleIdPrefix: com.yoakemae
  deploymentTarget:
    iOS: \"17.0\"
  xcodeVersion: \"15.0\"
  generateEmptyDirectories: true
  defaultConfig: Debug
  developmentLanguage: ja                    # ADD: Set Japanese as base language

settings:
  base:
    SWIFT_VERSION: \"5.9\"
    MARKETING_VERSION: \"1.0.0\"
    CURRENT_PROJECT_VERSION: \"1\"
    # ADD: Localization settings
    SWIFT_EMIT_LOC_STRINGS: \"YES\"

targets:
  YoakeMae:
    type: application
    platform: iOS
    sources:
      - path: YoakeMae
        excludes:
          - \"**/.DS_Store\"
    settings:
      base:
        INFOPLIST_FILE: YoakeMae/Resources/Info.plist
        PRODUCT_BUNDLE_IDENTIFIER: com.yoakemae.app
        DEVELOPMENT_TEAM: \"\"
        CODE_SIGN_STYLE: Automatic
    # ADD: Localization configuration
    info:
      properties:
        CFBundleLocalizations:
          - ja
          - en
```

### Step-by-Step Implementation Plan

#### Phase 1: Infrastructure Setup (Estimated: 30 min)

1. **Update project.yml**
   - Add `developmentLanguage: ja`
   - Add `SWIFT_EMIT_LOC_STRINGS: \"YES\"` to settings
   - Add `CFBundleLocalizations` array with `ja` and `en`

2. **Create String Catalog file**
   - Create `ios/YoakeMae/Resources/Localizable.xcstrings`
   - Initialize with JSON structure containing both languages

3. **Regenerate Xcode project**
   ```bash
   cd ios && make project
   ```

4. **Verify localization setup in Xcode**
   - Open project and confirm localization settings

---

#### Phase 2: Create Localization Helper (Estimated: 15 min)

Create a helper extension for consistent localization:

```swift
// ios/YoakeMae/Shared/Extensions/String+Localization.swift

import Foundation

extension String {
    /// Localized string accessor
    var localized: String {
        String(localized: LocalizedStringKey(self))
    }
    
    /// Localized string with arguments
    func localized(_ args: CVarArg...) -> String {
        String(format: String(localized: LocalizedStringKey(self)), arguments: args)
    }
}
```

---

#### Phase 3: Localize Enums and Models (Estimated: 1 hour)

Update enums to use localized strings:

**DrinkTypePreset** (`DrinkLogService.swift`):
```swift
var name: String {
    switch self {
    case .beer: return String(localized: \"drink_type_beer\")
    case .wine: return String(localized: \"drink_type_wine\")
    // ...
    }
}
```

**DrinkReasonPreset**:
```swift
var name: String {
    switch self {
    case .workStress: return String(localized: \"drink_reason_work_stress\")
    // ...
    }
}
```

**CorrelationStrength** (`TrendAnalysis.swift`):
```swift
enum CorrelationStrength: String, Codable, Sendable {
    case strong
    case moderate
    case weak
    case none
    case insufficient
    
    var localizedName: String {
        String(localized: LocalizedStringKey(\"correlation_\(self.rawValue)\"))
    }
}
```

**AnalysisPeriod**:
```swift
var label: String {
    switch self {
    case .week: return String(localized: \"period_week\")
    case .twoWeeks: return String(localized: \"period_two_weeks\")
    case .month: return String(localized: \"period_month\")
    }
}
```

#### Phase 6: Localize ViewModels (Estimated: 30 min)

**TrendAnalysisViewModel.swift**:
```swift
var dataPointMessage: String {
    guard let result = analysisResult else { return \"\" }
    if result.dataPointCount == 0 {
        return String(localized: \"data_point_none\")
    } else if result.dataPointCount < service.minimumDataPoints {
        return String(localized: \"data_point_insufficient \(result.dataPointCount) \(service.minimumDataPoints)\")
    }
    return String(localized: \"data_point_analyzing \(result.dataPointCount)\")
}
```

**DrinkLogViewModel.swift**:
```swift
successMessage = String(localized: \"drink_logged_success \(drinkType.icon) \(drinkType.name)\")
errorMessage = String(localized: \"error_load_logs\")
errorMessage = String(localized: \"error_log_drink\")
successMessage = String(localized: \"drink_logged_detailed_success\")
errorMessage = String(localized: \"error_delete_drink\")
```

#### Phase 9: Testing (Estimated: 1 hour)

1. **Build and run** with device language set to Japanese
2. **Switch device language** to English and verify all strings
3. **Test edge cases**: 
   - Strings with arguments (counts, percentages)
   - Pluralization if any
   - Chart labels and legends
4. **Run UI tests** in both languages

---

### Migration Strategy (Minimize Disruption)

1. **Do not break existing functionality** - Use SwiftUI's built-in localization which falls back to the key if translation is missing
2. **Incremental migration** - Start with shared components, then feature by feature
3. **Keep PR size manageable** - Consider splitting into multiple PRs:
   - PR 1: Infrastructure + Enums
   - PR 2: English Views (Dashboard, DrinkLog, SleepLog, MorningCondition, ContentView)
   - PR 3: Japanese Views (Settings, TrendAnalysis, Correlation)
   - PR 4: ViewModels and Services

---

### Critical Files for Implementation

- `/Users/yuichi.takada/workspace/sibukixxx/YoakeMae/ios/project.yml` - Must add localization configuration

    "content": "     1‚Üíimport Foundation
     2‚Üíimport SwiftData
     3‚Üí
     4‚Üí@MainActor
     5‚Üífinal class SwiftDataUserPreferencesRepository: UserPreferencesRepositoryProtocol {
     6‚Üí    private let modelContext: ModelContext
     7‚Üí    private let defaultId = \"default\"
     8‚Üí
     9‚Üí    init(modelContext: ModelContext) {
    10‚Üí        self.modelContext = modelContext
    11‚Üí    }
    12‚Üí
    13‚Üí    func get() async throws -> UserPreferencesEntity {
    14‚Üí        let id = defaultId
    15‚Üí        let predicate = #Predicate<UserPreferencesEntity> { entity in
    16‚Üí            entity.id == id
    17‚Üí        }
    18‚Üí
    19‚Üí        var descriptor = FetchDescriptor<UserPreferencesEntity>(predicate: predicate)
    20‚Üí        descriptor.fetchLimit = 1
    21‚Üí
    22‚Üí        if let existing = try modelContext.fetch(descriptor).first {
    23‚Üí            return existing
    24‚Üí        }
    25‚Üí
    26‚Üí        // Create default preferences
    27‚Üí        let defaults = UserPreferencesEntity()
    28‚Üí        modelContext.insert(defaults)
    29‚Üí        try modelContext.save()
    30‚Üí        return defaults
    31‚Üí    }
    32‚Üí
    33‚Üí    func save(_ entity: UserPreferencesEntity) async throws {
    34‚Üí        modelContext.insert(entity)
    35‚Üí        try modelContext.save()
    36‚Üí    }
    37‚Üí
    38‚Üí    func update(_ updateClosure: (UserPreferencesEntity) -> Void) async throws -> UserPreferencesEntity {
    39‚Üí        let preferences = try await get()
    40‚Üí        updateClosure(preferences)
    41‚Üí        preferences.update()
    42‚Üí        try modelContext.save()
    43‚Üí        return preferences
    44‚Üí    }
    45‚Üí
    46‚Üí    func reset() async throws -> UserPreferencesEntity {
    47‚Üí        // Delete existing
    48‚Üí        let id = defaultId
    49‚Üí        let predicate = #Predicate<UserPreferencesEntity> { entity in
    50‚Üí            entity.id == id
    51‚Üí        }
    52‚Üí
    53‚Üí        let descriptor = FetchDescriptor<UserPreferencesEntity>(predicate: predicate)
    54‚Üí        let existing = try modelContext.fetch(descriptor)
    55‚Üí        for entity in existing {
    56‚Üí            modelContext.delete(entity)
    57‚Üí        }
    58‚Üí
    59‚Üí        // Create new defaults
    60‚Üí        let defaults = UserPreferencesEntity()
    61‚Üí        modelContext.insert(defaults)
    62‚Üí        try modelContext.save()
    63‚Üí        return defaults
    64‚Üí    }
    65‚Üí}
    66‚Üí

- But many screens use **English** (Dashboard, Drink Log, Sleep Log, Morning Condition)
- **No systematic localization mechanism** - languages are hardcoded directly into code

  - Support additional languages

        "type": "text",
        "text": "Now I have a comprehensive understanding of the codebase. Let me compile the implementation plan.

## Implementation Plan: iOS Localization for YoakeMae

### Recommended Approach: String Catalogs (`.xcstrings`)

For iOS 17+, **String Catalogs** (`.xcstrings` format) is the recommended approach over traditional `.strings` files. Here is why:

**Advantages of String Catalogs:**
1. **Single file management** - One `.xcstrings` file contains all languages in JSON format
2. **Automatic string extraction** - Xcode automatically detects localizable strings from SwiftUI
3. **Built-in editor** - Xcode provides a visual editor with translation status tracking
4. **Better merge conflict handling** - JSON format is more git-friendly than binary `.strings` files
5. **Native SwiftUI integration** - Works seamlessly with `Text()`, `LocalizedStringKey`, and `String(localized:)`
6. **iOS 17+ is the minimum target** - This project already targets iOS 17.0

---

### File Structure for Localization Resources

```
ios/YoakeMae/
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Resources/
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Info.plist
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Assets.xcassets
‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Localizable.xcstrings        # NEW: Main string catalog
```

The String Catalog will contain translations organized by:
- **Source language**: Japanese (ja) - since Japanese is the primary language
- **Target language**: English (en)

---

### project.yml Changes Required

```yaml
name: YoakeMae
options:
  bundleIdPrefix: com.yoakemae
  deploymentTarget:
    iOS: \"17.0\"
  xcodeVersion: \"15.0\"
  generateEmptyDirectories: true
  defaultConfig: Debug
  developmentLanguage: ja                    # ADD: Set Japanese as base language

settings:
  base:
    SWIFT_VERSION: \"5.9\"
    MARKETING_VERSION: \"1.0.0\"
    CURRENT_PROJECT_VERSION: \"1\"
    # ADD: Localization settings
    SWIFT_EMIT_LOC_STRINGS: \"YES\"

targets:
  YoakeMae:
    type: application
    platform: iOS
    sources:
      - path: YoakeMae
        excludes:
          - \"**/.DS_Store\"
    settings:
      base:
        INFOPLIST_FILE: YoakeMae/Resources/Info.plist
        PRODUCT_BUNDLE_IDENTIFIER: com.yoakemae.app
        DEVELOPMENT_TEAM: \"\"
        CODE_SIGN_STYLE: Automatic
    # ADD: Localization configuration
    info:
      properties:
        CFBundleLocalizations:
          - ja
          - en
```

---

### Step-by-Step Implementation Plan

#### Phase 1: Infrastructure Setup (Estimated: 30 min)

1. **Update project.yml**
   - Add `developmentLanguage: ja`
   - Add `SWIFT_EMIT_LOC_STRINGS: \"YES\"` to settings
   - Add `CFBundleLocalizations` array with `ja` and `en`

2. **Create String Catalog file**
   - Create `ios/YoakeMae/Resources/Localizable.xcstrings`
   - Initialize with JSON structure containing both languages

3. **Regenerate Xcode project**
   ```bash
   cd ios && make project
   ```

4. **Verify localization setup in Xcode**
   - Open project and confirm localization settings

---

#### Phase 2: Create Localization Helper (Estimated: 15 min)

Create a helper extension for consistent localization:

```swift
// ios/YoakeMae/Shared/Extensions/String+Localization.swift

import Foundation

extension String {
    /// Localized string accessor
    var localized: String {
        String(localized: LocalizedStringKey(self))
    }
    
    /// Localized string with arguments
    func localized(_ args: CVarArg...) -> String {
        String(format: String(localized: LocalizedStringKey(self)), arguments: args)
    }
}
```

---

#### Phase 3: Localize Enums and Models (Estimated: 1 hour)

Update enums to use localized strings:

**DrinkTypePreset** (`DrinkLogService.swift`):
```swift
var name: String {
    switch self {
    case .beer: return String(localized: \"drink_type_beer\")
    case .wine: return String(localized: \"drink_type_wine\")
    // ...
    }
}
```

**DrinkReasonPreset**:
```swift
var name: String {
    switch self {
    case .workStress: return String(localized: \"drink_reason_work_stress\")
    // ...
    }
}
```

**CorrelationStrength** (`TrendAnalysis.swift`):
```swift
enum CorrelationStrength: String, Codable, Sendable {
    case strong
    case moderate
    case weak
    case none
    case insufficient
    
    var localizedName: String {
        String(localized: LocalizedStringKey(\"correlation_\(self.rawValue)\"))
    }
}
```

**AnalysisPeriod**:
```swift
var label: String {
    switch self {
    case .week: return String(localized: \"period_week\")
    case .twoWeeks: return String(localized: \"period_two_weeks\")
    case .month: return String(localized: \"period_month\")
    }
}
```

---

```swift
Text(\"sleep_good\") / Text(\"sleep_normal\") / Text(\"sleep_poor\") / Text(\"sleep_no_data\")
Text(\"avg_alcohol_label\")

// TimeWiseTrendSection
Text(\"time_wise_pattern_title\")
Text(\"time_range_night\") // Ê∑±Â§ú 0-6ÊôÇ
Text(\"time_range_morning\") // ÂçàÂâç 6-12ÊôÇ
Text(\"time_range_afternoon\") // ÂçàÂæå 12-18ÊôÇ
Text(\"time_range_evening\") // Â§ú 18-24ÊôÇ
Text(\"drink_count_format\") // \(count)Âõû
Text(\"avg_alcohol_format\") // Âπ≥Âùá %.1fg

// CorrelationSection
Text(\"correlation_title\")
Text(\"sleep_quality_correlation\")
Text(\"morning_condition_correlation\")
Text(\"correlation_coefficient\")
Text(\"analysis_result_title\")
```

**LocalTrendAnalysisService.swift** - Dynamic interpretation messages:
```swift
// These need to use String(localized:) with argument interpolation
String(localized: \"interpretation_strong_positive_sleep\")
String(localized: \"interpretation_strong_negative_sleep\")
String(localized: \"interpretation_moderate_sleep\")
String(localized: \"interpretation_weak_sleep\")
String(localized: \"interpretation_none_sleep\")
String(localized: \"interpretation_insufficient_sleep_data\")
// Similar for morning condition
String(localized: \"interpretation_analysis_insufficient\")
```

---

#### Phase 6: Localize ViewModels (Estimated: 30 min)

**TrendAnalysisViewModel.swift**:
```swift
var dataPointMessage: String {
    guard let result = analysisResult else { return \"\" }
    if result.dataPointCount == 0 {
        return String(localized: \"data_point_none\")
    } else if result.dataPointCount < service.minimumDataPoints {
        return String(localized: \"data_point_insufficient \(result.dataPointCount) \(service.minimumDataPoints)\")
    }
    return String(localized: \"data_point_analyzing \(result.dataPointCount)\")
}
```

**DrinkLogViewModel.swift**:
```swift
successMessage = String(localized: \"drink_logged_success \(drinkType.icon) \(drinkType.name)\")
errorMessage = String(localized: \"error_load_logs\")
errorMessage = String(localized: \"error_log_drink\")
successMessage = String(localized: \"drink_logged_detailed_success\")
errorMessage = String(localized: \"error_delete_drink\")
```

---

#### Phase 7: Shared Components (Estimated: 15 min)

**ErrorView.swift**:
```swift
Button(String(localized: \"retry_button\")) {
    retryAction()
}
```

**LoadingView.swift**: Already takes message as parameter, no change needed.

---

#### Phase 8: Populate String Catalog (Estimated: 1-2 hours)

Create the `Localizable.xcstrings` file with all keys. Example structure:

```json
{
  \"sourceLanguage\" : \"ja\",
  \"strings\" : {
    \"tab_home\" : {
      \"extractionState\" : \"manual\",
      \"localizations\" : {
        \"ja\" : {
          \"stringUnit\" : {
            \"state\" : \"translated\",
            \"value\" : \"„Éõ„Éº„É†\"
          }

```

#### Phase 9: Testing (Estimated: 1 hour)

1. **Build and run** with device language set to Japanese
2. **Switch device language** to English and verify all strings
3. **Test edge cases**: 
   - Strings with arguments (counts, percentages)
   - Pluralization if any
   - Chart labels and legends
4. **Run UI tests** in both languages

---

### Migration Strategy (Minimize Disruption)

1. **Do not break existing functionality** - Use SwiftUI's built-in localization which falls back to the key if translation is missing
2. **Incremental migration** - Start with shared components, then feature by feature
3. **Keep PR size manageable** - Consider splitting into multiple PRs:
   - PR 1: Infrastructure + Enums
   - PR 2: English Views (Dashboard, DrinkLog, SleepLog, MorningCondition, ContentView)
   - PR 3: Japanese Views (Settings, TrendAnalysis, Correlation)
   - PR 4: ViewModels and Services

---

     4‚Üí@MainActor
     5‚Üífinal class LocalTrendAnalysisService: TrendAnalysisServiceProtocol {
     6‚Üí
     7‚Üí    // MARK: - Dependencies
     8‚Üí
     9‚Üí    private let drinkLogRepository: DrinkLogRepositoryProtocol
    10‚Üí    private let sleepLogRepository: SleepLogRepositoryProtocol

    16‚Üí

    21‚Üí        (6, 12, \"ÂçàÂâç 6-12ÊôÇ\"),
    22‚Üí        (12, 18, \"ÂçàÂæå 12-18ÊôÇ\"),
    23‚Üí        (18, 24, \"Â§ú 18-24ÊôÇ\")
    24‚Üí    ]
    25‚Üí
    26‚Üí    // MARK: - Initialization
    27‚Üí
    28‚Üí    init(
    29‚Üí        drinkLogRepository: DrinkLogRepositoryProtocol,
    30‚Üí        sleepLogRepository: SleepLogRepositoryProtocol,
    31‚Üí        morningConditionRepository: MorningConditionRepositoryProtocol
    32‚Üí    ) {

    34‚Üí        self.sleepLogRepository = sleepLogRepository
    35‚Üí        self.morningConditionRepository = morningConditionRepository

    39‚Üí
    40‚Üí    func analyze(days: Int) async throws -> TrendAnalysisResult {
    41‚Üí        async let dayWise = getDayWiseTrends(days: days)
    42‚Üí        async let timeWise = getTimeWiseTrends(days: days)
    43‚Üí        async let correlationData = getCorrelation(days: days)
    44‚Üí
    45‚Üí        let drinkLogCount = try await drinkLogRepository.count()
    46‚Üí
    47‚Üí        return try await TrendAnalysisResult(
    48‚Üí            dayWiseTrends: dayWise,
    49‚Üí            timeWiseTrends: timeWise,

    53‚Üí        )
    54‚Üí    }
    55‚Üí
    56‚Üí    func getDayWiseTrends(days: Int) async throws -> [DayWiseTrend] {
    57‚Üí        let calendar = Calendar.current
    58‚Üí        let today = calendar.startOfDay(for: Date())
    59‚Üí
    60‚Üí        // ÊõúÊó•„Åî„Å®„ÅÆÁµ±Ë®à„ÇíÂàùÊúüÂåñÔºà1=Êó•Êõú ... 7=ÂúüÊõúÔºâ
    61‚Üí        var weekdayStats: [Int: WeekdayStats] = [:]
    62‚Üí        for weekday in 1...7 {
    63‚Üí            weekdayStats[weekday] = WeekdayStats()
    64‚Üí        }
    65‚Üí
    66‚Üí        // ÈÅéÂéªNÊó•Èñì„ÅÆ„Éá„Éº„Çø„ÇíÈõÜË®à
    67‚Üí        for dayOffset in 0..<days {
    68‚Üí            guard let date = calendar.date(byAdding: .day, value: -dayOffset, to: today) else {
    69‚Üí                continue
    70‚Üí            }
    71‚Üí            let weekday = calendar.component(.weekday, from: date)
    72‚Üí
    73‚Üí            let drinkLogs = try await drinkLogRepository.fetchByDate(date)
    74‚Üí            let sleepLog = try await sleepLogRepository.fetchByDate(date)
    75‚Üí            let morningLog = try await morningConditionRepository.fetchByDate(date)
    76‚Üí
    77‚Üí            var stats = weekdayStats[weekday]!
    78‚Üí            stats.totalDays += 1
    79‚Üí
    80‚Üí            if !drinkLogs.isEmpty {
    81‚Üí                stats.drinkingDays += 1
    82‚Üí            }
    83‚Üí            stats.drinkCount += drinkLogs.count
    84‚Üí            stats.totalAlcohol += drinkLogs.reduce(0.0) { $0 + $1.calculateAlcoholAmount() }
    85‚Üí
    86‚Üí            if let sleep = sleepLog {
    87‚Üí                stats.sleepScores.append(sleep.averageScore)
    88‚Üí            }
    89‚Üí            if let morning = morningLog {
    90‚Üí                stats.morningScores.append(morning.overallScore)
    91‚Üí            }
    92‚Üí
    93‚Üí            weekdayStats[weekday] = stats
    94‚Üí        }
    95‚Üí
    96‚Üí        // ÁµêÊûú„ÇíÁîüÊàê
    97‚Üí        let weekdaySymbols = calendar.shortWeekdaySymbols
    98‚Üí
    99‚Üí        return (1...7).map { weekday in
   100‚Üí            let stats = weekdayStats[weekday]!
   101‚Üí
   102‚Üí            return DayWiseTrend(
   103‚Üí                weekday: weekday,
   104‚Üí                weekdayName: weekdaySymbols[weekday - 1],
   105‚Üí                avgDrinkCount: stats.totalDays > 0
   106‚Üí                    ? Double(stats.drinkCount) / Double(stats.totalDays)
   107‚Üí                    : 0,
   108‚Üí                avgAlcohol: stats.totalDays > 0
   109‚Üí                    ? stats.totalAlcohol / Double(stats.totalDays)
   110‚Üí                    : 0,
   111‚Üí                drinkingRate: stats.totalDays > 0
   112‚Üí                    ? Double(stats.drinkingDays) / Double(stats.totalDays)
   113‚Üí                    : 0,
   114‚Üí                avgSleepScore: stats.sleepScores.isEmpty
   115‚Üí                    ? nil
   116‚Üí                    : stats.sleepScores.reduce(0, +) / Double(stats.sleepScores.count),
   117‚Üí                avgMorningScore: stats.morningScores.isEmpty
   118‚Üí                    ? nil
   119‚Üí                    : stats.morningScores.reduce(0, +) / Double(stats.morningScores.count)
   120‚Üí            )
   121‚Üí        }
   122‚Üí    }
   123‚Üí
   124‚Üí    func getTimeWiseTrends(days: Int) async throws -> [TimeWiseTrend] {
   125‚Üí        let calendar = Calendar.current
   126‚Üí        let today = calendar.startOfDay(for: Date())
   127‚Üí
   128‚Üí        // ÊôÇÈñìÂ∏Ø„Åî„Å®„ÅÆÁµ±Ë®à„ÇíÂàùÊúüÂåñ
   129‚Üí        var rangeStats: [(range: String, startHour: Int, endHour: Int, count: Int, alcohol: Double)] =
   130‚Üí            timeRanges.map { ($0.label, $0.start, $0.end, 0, 0.0) }
   131‚Üí
   132‚Üí        // ÈÅéÂéªNÊó•Èñì„ÅÆ„Éá„Éº„Çø„ÇíÈõÜË®à
   133‚Üí        for dayOffset in 0..<days {
   134‚Üí            guard let date = calendar.date(byAdding: .day, value: -dayOffset, to: today) else {
   135‚Üí                continue
   136‚Üí            }
   137‚Üí            let drinkLogs = try await drinkLogRepository.fetchByDate(date)
   138‚Üí
   139‚Üí            for log in drinkLogs {
   140‚Üí                let hour = calendar.component(.hour, from: log.startedAt)
   141‚Üí
   142‚Üí                for (index, range) in timeRanges.enumerated() {
   143‚Üí                    if hour >= range.start && hour < range.end {
   144‚Üí                        rangeStats[index].count += 1
   145‚Üí                        rangeStats[index].alcohol += log.calculateAlcoholAmount()
   146‚Üí                        break
   147‚Üí                    }
   148‚Üí                }
   149‚Üí            }
   150‚Üí        }
   151‚Üí
   152‚Üí        // ÂÖ®È£≤ÈÖíÂõûÊï∞
   153‚Üí        let totalCount = rangeStats.reduce(0) { $0 + $1.count }
   154‚Üí
   155‚Üí        return rangeStats.map { stat in
   156‚Üí            TimeWiseTrend(
   157‚Üí                timeRange: stat.range,
   158‚Üí                startHour: stat.startHour,
   159‚Üí                endHour: stat.endHour,
   160‚Üí                drinkCount: stat.count,
   161‚Üí                avgAlcohol: stat.count > 0 ? stat.alcohol / Double(stat.count) : 0,
   162‚Üí                frequency: totalCount > 0 ? Double(stat.count) / Double(totalCount) : 0
   163‚Üí            )
   164‚Üí        }
   165‚Üí    }
   166‚Üí
   167‚Üí    func getCorrelation(days: Int) async throws -> CorrelationData {
   168‚Üí        let calendar = Calendar.current
   169‚Üí        let today = calendar.startOfDay(for: Date())
   170‚Üí
   171‚Üí        var alcoholSleepPairs: [(Double, Double)] = []
   172‚Üí        var alcoholMorningPairs: [(Double, Double)] = []
   173‚Üí
   174‚Üí        // ÈÅéÂéªNÊó•Èñì„ÅÆ„Éá„Éº„Çø„ÇíÈõÜË®à
   175‚Üí        // ÂâçÊó•„ÅÆ„Ç¢„É´„Ç≥„Éº„É´Èáè„Å®ÁøåÊó•„ÅÆÁù°Áú†/Êúù„Ç≥„É≥„Éá„Ç£„Ç∑„Éß„É≥„ÅÆÁõ∏Èñ¢„ÇíË¶ã„Çã
   176‚Üí        for dayOffset in 1..<days {
   177‚Üí            guard let date = calendar.date(byAdding: .day, value: -dayOffset, to: today),
   178‚Üí                  let prevDate = calendar.date(byAdding: .day, value: -1, to: date) else {
   179‚Üí                continue
   180‚Üí            }
   181‚Üí
   182‚Üí            // ÂâçÊó•„ÅÆ„Ç¢„É´„Ç≥„Éº„É´Èáè
   183‚Üí            let alcohol = try await drinkLogRepository.totalAlcoholByDate(prevDate)
   184‚Üí
   185‚Üí            // ÂΩìÊó•„ÅÆÁù°Áú†„ÉªÊúù„Ç≥„É≥„Éá„Ç£„Ç∑„Éß„É≥
   186‚Üí            if let sleepLog = try await sleepLogRepository.fetchByDate(date) {
   187‚Üí                alcoholSleepPairs.append((alcohol, sleepLog.averageScore))
   188‚Üí            }
   189‚Üí            if let morningLog = try await morningConditionRepository.fetchByDate(date) {
   190‚Üí                alcoholMorningPairs.append((alcohol, morningLog.overallScore))
   191‚Üí            }
   192‚Üí        }
   193‚Üí
   194‚Üí        let alcoholVsSleep = calculatePearsonCorrelation(alcoholSleepPairs)
   195‚Üí        let alcoholVsMorning = calculatePearsonCorrelation(alcoholMorningPairs)
   196‚Üí
   197‚Üí        return CorrelationData(
   198‚Üí            alcoholVsSleep: alcoholVsSleep,
   199‚Üí            alcoholVsMorning: alcoholVsMorning,
   200‚Üí            interpretations: generateInterpretations(
   201‚Üí                alcoholVsSleep: alcoholVsSleep,
   202‚Üí                alcoholVsMorning: alcoholVsMorning,
   203‚Üí                sleepDataCount: alcoholSleepPairs.count,
   204‚Üí                morningDataCount: alcoholMorningPairs.count
   205‚Üí            )
   206‚Üí        )
   207‚Üí    }
   208‚Üí
   209‚Üí    // MARK: - Private Helpers
   210‚Üí
   211‚Üí    /// „Éî„Ç¢„ÇΩ„É≥Áõ∏Èñ¢‰øÇÊï∞„ÇíË®àÁÆó
   212‚Üí    private func calculatePearsonCorrelation(_ pairs: [(Double, Double)]) -> Double? {
   213‚Üí        guard pairs.count >= 5 else { return nil }
   214‚Üí
   215‚Üí        let n = Double(pairs.count)
   216‚Üí        let sumX = pairs.reduce(0) { $0 + $1.0 }
   217‚Üí        let sumY = pairs.reduce(0) { $0 + $1.1 }
   218‚Üí        let sumXY = pairs.reduce(0) { $0 + $1.0 * $1.1 }
   219‚Üí        let sumX2 = pairs.reduce(0) { $0 + $1.0 * $1.0 }
   220‚Üí        let sumY2 = pairs.reduce(0) { $0 + $1.1 * $1.1 }
   221‚Üí
   222‚Üí        let numerator = n * sumXY - sumX * sumY
   223‚Üí        let denominator = sqrt((n * sumX2 - sumX * sumX) * (n * sumY2 - sumY * sumY))
   224‚Üí
   225‚Üí        guard denominator != 0 else { return nil }
   226‚Üí        return numerator / denominator
   227‚Üí    }
   228‚Üí
   229‚Üí    /// Áõ∏Èñ¢„ÅÆËß£Èáà„ÉÜ„Ç≠„Çπ„Éà„ÇíÁîüÊàê
   230‚Üí    private func generateInterpretations(
   231‚Üí        alcoholVsSleep: Double?,
   232‚Üí        alcoholVsMorning: Double?,
   233‚Üí        sleepDataCount: Int,
   234‚Üí        morningDataCount: Int
   235‚Üí    ) -> [String] {
   236‚Üí        var interpretations: [String] = []
   237‚Üí
   238‚Üí        // Áù°Áú†„Å®„ÅÆÁõ∏Èñ¢„ÅÆËß£Èáà
   239‚Üí        if let sleepCorr = alcoholVsSleep {
   240‚Üí            let strength = CorrelationStrength.from(sleepCorr)
   241‚Üí            let direction = sleepCorr > 0 ? \"Ê≠£\" : \"Ë≤†\"
   242‚Üí
   243‚Üí            switch strength {
   244‚Üí            case .strong:
   245‚Üí                interpretations.append(\"È£≤ÈÖíÈáè„Å®Áù°Áú†„ÅÆË≥™„Å´„ÅØ\(direction)„ÅÆÂº∑„ÅÑÁõ∏Èñ¢„Åå„ÅÇ„Çä„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ\")
   246‚Üí                if sleepCorr > 0 {
   247‚Üí                    interpretations.append(\"È£≤ÈÖíÈáè„ÅåÂ§ö„ÅÑÊó•„ÅÆÁøåÊó•„ÅØÁù°Áú†„Çπ„Ç≥„Ç¢„ÅåÊÇ™Âåñ„Åô„ÇãÂÇæÂêë„Åå„ÅÇ„Çä„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ\")
   248‚Üí                }
   249‚Üí            case .moderate:
   250‚Üí                interpretations.append(\"È£≤ÈÖíÈáè„Å®Áù°Áú†„ÅÆË≥™„Å´„ÅØ\(direction)„ÅÆ‰∏≠Á®ãÂ∫¶„ÅÆÁõ∏Èñ¢„Åå„ÅÇ„Çä„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ\")
   251‚Üí            case .weak:
   252‚Üí                interpretations.append(\"È£≤ÈÖíÈáè„Å®Áù°Áú†„ÅÆË≥™„Å´„ÅØÂº±„ÅÑÁõ∏Èñ¢„ÅåË¶ã„Çâ„Çå„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ\")
   253‚Üí            case .none:
   254‚Üí                interpretations.append(\"È£≤ÈÖíÈáè„Å®Áù°Áú†„ÅÆË≥™„Å´ÊòéÁ¢∫„Å™Áõ∏Èñ¢„ÅØË¶ã„Çâ„Çå„Åæ„Åõ„Çì„ÄÇ\")
   255‚Üí            case .insufficient:
   256‚Üí                break
   257‚Üí            }
   258‚Üí        } else if sleepDataCount < 5 {
   259‚Üí            interpretations.append(\"Áù°Áú†„Éá„Éº„Çø„Åå‰∏çË∂≥„Åó„Å¶„ÅÑ„Åæ„ÅôÔºà\(sleepDataCount)Êó•ÂàÜÔºâ„ÄÇ5Êó•‰ª•‰∏ä„ÅÆ„Éá„Éº„Çø„ÅåÂøÖË¶Å„Åß„Åô„ÄÇ\")
   260‚Üí        }

   262‚Üí        // Êúù„Ç≥„É≥„Éá„Ç£„Ç∑„Éß„É≥„Å®„ÅÆÁõ∏Èñ¢„ÅÆËß£Èáà
   263‚Üí        if let morningCorr = alcoholVsMorning {
   264‚Üí            let strength = CorrelationStrength.from(morningCorr)
   265‚Üí            let direction = morningCorr > 0 ? \"Ê≠£\" : \"Ë≤†\"

    56‚Üí    func getDayWiseTrends(days: Int) async throws -> [DayWiseTrend] {
    57‚Üí        let calendar = Calendar.current
    58‚Üí        let today = calendar.startOfDay(for: Date())
    59‚Üí
    60‚Üí        // ÊõúÊó•„Åî„Å®„ÅÆÁµ±Ë®à„ÇíÂàùÊúüÂåñÔºà1=Êó•Êõú ... 7=ÂúüÊõúÔºâ
    61‚Üí        var weekdayStats: [Int: WeekdayStats] = [:]
    62‚Üí        for weekday in 1...7 {
    63‚Üí            weekdayStats[weekday] = WeekdayStats()
    64‚Üí        }
    65‚Üí
    66‚Üí        // ÈÅéÂéªNÊó•Èñì„ÅÆ„Éá„Éº„Çø„ÇíÈõÜË®à
    67‚Üí        for dayOffset in 0..<days {
    68‚Üí            guard let date = calendar.date(byAdding: .day, value: -dayOffset, to: today) else {
    69‚Üí                continue
    70‚Üí            }
    71‚Üí            let weekday = calendar.component(.weekday, from: date)
    72‚Üí
    73‚Üí            let drinkLogs = try await drinkLogRepository.fetchByDate(date)
    74‚Üí            let sleepLog = try await sleepLogRepository.fetchByDate(date)
    75‚Üí            let morningLog = try await morningConditionRepository.fetchByDate(date)
    76‚Üí
    77‚Üí            var stats = weekdayStats[weekday]!

    79‚Üí
    80‚Üí            if !drinkLogs.isEmpty {
    81‚Üí                stats.drinkingDays += 1
    82‚Üí            }

    84‚Üí            stats.totalAlcohol += drinkLogs.reduce(0.0) { $0 + $1.calculateAlcoholAmount() }
    85‚Üí
    86‚Üí            if let sleep = sleepLog {
    87‚Üí                stats.sleepScores.append(sleep.averageScore)
    88‚Üí            }
    89‚Üí            if let morning = morningLog {
    90‚Üí                stats.morningScores.append(morning.overallScore)
    91‚Üí            }
    92‚Üí
    93‚Üí            weekdayStats[weekday] = stats
    94‚Üí        }
    95‚Üí
    96‚Üí        // ÁµêÊûú„ÇíÁîüÊàê
    97‚Üí        let weekdaySymbols = calendar.shortWeekdaySymbols
    98‚Üí
    99‚Üí        return (1...7).map { weekday in
   100‚Üí            let stats = weekdayStats[weekday]!
   101‚Üí
   102‚Üí            return DayWiseTrend(
   103‚Üí                weekday: weekday,
   104‚Üí                weekdayName: weekdaySymbols[weekday - 1],
   105‚Üí                avgDrinkCount: stats.totalDays > 0
   106‚Üí                    ? Double(stats.drinkCount) / Double(stats.totalDays)
   107‚Üí                    : 0,
   108‚Üí                avgAlcohol: stats.totalDays > 0
   109‚Üí                    ? stats.totalAlcohol / Double(stats.totalDays)
   110‚Üí                    : 0,
   111‚Üí                drinkingRate: stats.totalDays > 0
   112‚Üí                    ? Double(stats.drinkingDays) / Double(stats.totalDays)
   113‚Üí                    : 0,
   114‚Üí                avgSleepScore: stats.sleepScores.isEmpty
   115‚Üí                    ? nil
   116‚Üí                    : stats.sleepScores.reduce(0, +) / Double(stats.sleepScores.count),
   117‚Üí                avgMorningScore: stats.morningScores.isEmpty
   118‚Üí                    ? nil
   119‚Üí                    : stats.morningScores.reduce(0, +) / Double(stats.morningScores.count)
   120‚Üí            )
   121‚Üí        }
   122‚Üí    }

   124‚Üí    func getTimeWiseTrends(days: Int) async throws -> [TimeWiseTrend] {
   125‚Üí        let calendar = Calendar.current
   126‚Üí        let today = calendar.startOfDay(for: Date())
   127‚Üí
   128‚Üí        // ÊôÇÈñìÂ∏Ø„Åî„Å®„ÅÆÁµ±Ë®à„ÇíÂàùÊúüÂåñ
   129‚Üí        var rangeStats: [(range: String, startHour: Int, endHour: Int, count: Int, alcohol: Double)] =
   130‚Üí            timeRanges.map { ($0.label, $0.start, $0.end, 0, 0.0) }
   131‚Üí
   132‚Üí        // ÈÅéÂéªNÊó•Èñì„ÅÆ„Éá„Éº„Çø„ÇíÈõÜË®à
   133‚Üí        for dayOffset in 0..<days {
   134‚Üí            guard let date = calendar.date(byAdding: .day, value: -dayOffset, to: today) else {
   135‚Üí                continue
   136‚Üí            }
   137‚Üí            let drinkLogs = try await drinkLogRepository.fetchByDate(date)
   138‚Üí
   139‚Üí            for log in drinkLogs {
   140‚Üí                let hour = calendar.component(.hour, from: log.startedAt)
   141‚Üí
   142‚Üí                for (index, range) in timeRanges.enumerated() {
   143‚Üí                    if hour >= range.start && hour < range.end {
   144‚Üí                        rangeStats[index].count += 1
   145‚Üí                        rangeStats[index].alcohol += log.calculateAlcoholAmount()
   146‚Üí                        break
   147‚Üí                    }
   148‚Üí                }
   149‚Üí            }
   150‚Üí        }
   151‚Üí
   152‚Üí        // ÂÖ®È£≤ÈÖíÂõûÊï∞
   153‚Üí        let totalCount = rangeStats.reduce(0) { $0 + $1.count }
   154‚Üí
   155‚Üí        return rangeStats.map { stat in
   156‚Üí            TimeWiseTrend(
   157‚Üí                timeRange: stat.range,
   158‚Üí                startHour: stat.startHour,
   159‚Üí                endHour: stat.endHour,
   160‚Üí                drinkCount: stat.count,
   161‚Üí                avgAlcohol: stat.count > 0 ? stat.alcohol / Double(stat.count) : 0,
   162‚Üí                frequency: totalCount > 0 ? Double(stat.count) / Double(totalCount) : 0
   163‚Üí            )
   164‚Üí        }
   165‚Üí    }
   166‚Üí
   167‚Üí    func getCorrelation(days: Int) async throws -> CorrelationData {
   168‚Üí        let calendar = Calendar.current
   169‚Üí        let today = calendar.startOfDay(for: Date())
   170‚Üí
   171‚Üí        var alcoholSleepPairs: [(Double, Double)] = []
   172‚Üí        var alcoholMorningPairs: [(Double, Double)] = []
   173‚Üí
   174‚Üí        // ÈÅéÂéªNÊó•Èñì„ÅÆ„Éá„Éº„Çø„ÇíÈõÜË®à
   175‚Üí        // ÂâçÊó•„ÅÆ„Ç¢„É´„Ç≥„Éº„É´Èáè„Å®ÁøåÊó•„ÅÆÁù°Áú†/Êúù„Ç≥„É≥„Éá„Ç£„Ç∑„Éß„É≥„ÅÆÁõ∏Èñ¢„ÇíË¶ã„Çã
   176‚Üí        for dayOffset in 1..<days {
   177‚Üí            guard let date = calendar.date(byAdding: .day, value: -dayOffset, to: today),
   178‚Üí                  let prevDate = calendar.date(byAdding: .day, value: -1, to: date) else {
   179‚Üí                continue
   180‚Üí            }
   181‚Üí
   182‚Üí            // ÂâçÊó•„ÅÆ„Ç¢„É´„Ç≥„Éº„É´Èáè
   183‚Üí            let alcohol = try await drinkLogRepository.totalAlcoholByDate(prevDate)
   184‚Üí
   185‚Üí            // ÂΩìÊó•„ÅÆÁù°Áú†„ÉªÊúù„Ç≥„É≥„Éá„Ç£„Ç∑„Éß„É≥
   186‚Üí            if let sleepLog = try await sleepLogRepository.fetchByDate(date) {
   187‚Üí                alcoholSleepPairs.append((alcohol, sleepLog.averageScore))
   188‚Üí            }
   189‚Üí            if let morningLog = try await morningConditionRepository.fetchByDate(date) {
   190‚Üí                alcoholMorningPairs.append((alcohol, morningLog.overallScore))
   191‚Üí            }
   192‚Üí        }
   193‚Üí
   194‚Üí        let alcoholVsSleep = calculatePearsonCorrelation(alcoholSleepPairs)
   195‚Üí        let alcoholVsMorning = calculatePearsonCorrelation(alcoholMorningPairs)
   196‚Üí
   197‚Üí        return CorrelationData(
   198‚Üí            alcoholVsSleep: alcoholVsSleep,
   199‚Üí            alcoholVsMorning: alcoholVsMorning,
   200‚Üí            interpretations: generateInterpretations(
   201‚Üí                alcoholVsSleep: alcoholVsSleep,
   202‚Üí                alcoholVsMorning: alcoholVsMorning,
   203‚Üí                sleepDataCount: alcoholSleepPairs.count,
   204‚Üí                morningDataCount: alcoholMorningPairs.count
   205‚Üí            )
   206‚Üí        )
   207‚Üí    }
   208‚Üí
   209‚Üí    // MARK: - Private Helpers
   210‚Üí
   211‚Üí    /// „Éî„Ç¢„ÇΩ„É≥Áõ∏Èñ¢‰øÇÊï∞„ÇíË®àÁÆó
   212‚Üí    private func calculatePearsonCorrelation(_ pairs: [(Double, Double)]) -> Double? {
   213‚Üí        guard pairs.count >= 5 else { return nil }
   214‚Üí
   215‚Üí        let n = Double(pairs.count)
   216‚Üí        let sumX = pairs.reduce(0) { $0 + $1.0 }
   217‚Üí        let sumY = pairs.reduce(0) { $0 + $1.1 }
   218‚Üí        let sumXY = pairs.reduce(0) { $0 + $1.0 * $1.1 }
   219‚Üí        let sumX2 = pairs.reduce(0) { $0 + $1.0 * $1.0 }
   220‚Üí        let sumY2 = pairs.reduce(0) { $0 + $1.1 * $1.1 }
   221‚Üí
   222‚Üí        let numerator = n * sumXY - sumX * sumY
   223‚Üí        let denominator = sqrt((n * sumX2 - sumX * sumX) * (n * sumY2 - sumY * sumY))
   224‚Üí
   225‚Üí        guard denominator != 0 else { return nil }
   226‚Üí        return numerator / denominator
   227‚Üí    }
   228‚Üí
   229‚Üí    /// Áõ∏Èñ¢„ÅÆËß£Èáà„ÉÜ„Ç≠„Çπ„Éà„ÇíÁîüÊàê
   230‚Üí    private func generateInterpretations(
   231‚Üí        alcoholVsSleep: Double?,
   232‚Üí        alcoholVsMorning: Double?,
   233‚Üí        sleepDataCount: Int,
   234‚Üí        morningDataCount: Int
   235‚Üí    ) -> [String] {
   236‚Üí        var interpretations: [String] = []
   237‚Üí
   238‚Üí        // Áù°Áú†„Å®„ÅÆÁõ∏Èñ¢„ÅÆËß£Èáà
   239‚Üí        if let sleepCorr = alcoholVsSleep {
   240‚Üí            let strength = CorrelationStrength.from(sleepCorr)
   241‚Üí            let direction = sleepCorr > 0 ? \"Ê≠£\" : \"Ë≤†\"
   242‚Üí
   243‚Üí            switch strength {
   244‚Üí            case .strong:
   245‚Üí                interpretations.append(\"È£≤ÈÖíÈáè„Å®Áù°Áú†„ÅÆË≥™„Å´„ÅØ\(direction)„ÅÆÂº∑„ÅÑÁõ∏Èñ¢„Åå„ÅÇ„Çä„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ\")
   246‚Üí                if sleepCorr > 0 {
   247‚Üí                    interpretations.append(\"È£≤ÈÖíÈáè„ÅåÂ§ö„ÅÑÊó•„ÅÆÁøåÊó•„ÅØÁù°Áú†„Çπ„Ç≥„Ç¢„ÅåÊÇ™Âåñ„Åô„ÇãÂÇæÂêë„Åå„ÅÇ„Çä„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ\")
   248‚Üí                }
   249‚Üí            case .moderate:
   250‚Üí                interpretations.append(\"È£≤ÈÖíÈáè„Å®Áù°Áú†„ÅÆË≥™„Å´„ÅØ\(direction)„ÅÆ‰∏≠Á®ãÂ∫¶„ÅÆÁõ∏Èñ¢„Åå„ÅÇ„Çä„Åæ„Åô„ÄÇ\")
   251‚Üí            case .weak:

   251‚Üí        case .danger: return .red
   252‚Üí        }

   255‚Üí    private func formatDate(_ date: Date) -> String {

   258‚Üí        return formatter.localizedString(for: date, relativeTo: Date())

   320‚Üístruct DayColumn: View {
   321‚Üí    let summary: DailySummary
   322‚Üí    let dayIndex: Int
   323‚Üí
   324‚Üí    var body: some View {
   325‚Üí        VStack(spacing: 4) {
   326‚Üí            Text(dayLabel)
   327‚Üí                .font(.caption2)
   328‚Üí                .foregroundColor(.secondary)
   329‚Üí
   330‚Üí            Rectangle()
   331‚Üí                .fill(barColor)
   332‚Üí                .frame(height: barHeight)
   333‚Üí                .frame(maxWidth: .infinity)
   334‚Üí                .cornerRadius(4)
   335‚Üí
   336‚Üí            Text(summary.drinkCount > 0 ? \"\(summary.drinkCount)\" : \"-\")
   337‚Üí                .font(.caption2)
   338‚Üí                .foregroundColor(.secondary)
   339‚Üí        }
   340‚Üí    }
   341‚Üí
   342‚Üí    private var dayLabel: String {
   343‚Üí        let days = [\"Sun\", \"Mon\", \"Tue\", \"Wed\", \"Thu\", \"Fri\", \"Sat\"]
   344‚Üí        let calendar = Calendar.current
   345‚Üí        let weekday = calendar.component(.weekday, from: Date()) - 1
   346‚Üí        let adjustedIndex = (weekday - 6 + dayIndex + 7) % 7
   347‚Üí        return days[adjustedIndex]
   348‚Üí    }
   349‚Üí
   350‚Üí    private var barHeight: CGFloat {
   351‚Üí        let maxHeight: CGFloat = 60
   352‚Üí        let minHeight: CGFloat = 8
   353‚Üí        guard summary.drinkCount > 0 else { return minHeight }
   354‚Üí        return min(maxHeight, max(minHeight, CGFloat(summary.drinkCount) * 15))
   355‚Üí    }
   356‚Üí
   357‚Üí    private var barColor: Color {
   358‚Üí        if summary.hasAlert {
   359‚Üí            return .red
   360‚Üí        }
   361‚Üí        switch summary.drinkCount {
   362‚Üí        case 0: return .gray.opacity(0.3)
   363‚Üí        case 1...2: return .green
   364‚Üí        case 3: return .yellow
   365‚Üí        case 4: return .orange
   366‚Üí        default: return .red
   367‚Üí        }
   368‚Üí    }
   369‚Üí}
   370‚Üí
   371‚Üístruct WeeklyStatItem: View {
   372‚Üí    let label: String
   373‚Üí    let value: String
   374‚Üí
   375‚Üí    var body: some View {
   376‚Üí        VStack(spacing: 4) {

   378‚Üí                .font(.headline)
   379‚Üí            Text(label)
   380‚Üí                .font(.caption)
   381‚Üí                .foregroundColor(.secondary)
   382‚Üí        }
   383‚Üí    }
   384‚Üí}

   239‚Üí
   240‚Üístruct ConditionScoreSelector: View {
   241‚Üí    let title: String
   242‚Üí    let description: String
   243‚Üí    @Binding var value: Int
   244‚Üí    let isRequired: Bool
   245‚Üí    let minLabel: String
   246‚Üí    let maxLabel: String
   247‚Üí
   248‚Üí    var body: some View {
   249‚Üí        VStack(alignment: .leading, spacing: 8) {
   250‚Üí            HStack {
   251‚Üí                Text(title)
   252‚Üí                    .font(.subheadline)
   253‚Üí                    .fontWeight(.medium)
   254‚Üí                if isRequired {
   255‚Üí                    Text(\"*\")
   256‚Üí                        .foregroundColor(.red)
   257‚Üí                }
   258‚Üí                Spacer()
   259‚Üí                Text(\"\(value)\")
   260‚Üí                    .font(.headline)
   261‚Üí                    .foregroundColor(colorForValue(value))
   262‚Üí            }
   263‚Üí
   264‚Üí            Text(description)
   265‚Üí                .font(.caption)
   266‚Üí                .foregroundColor(.secondary)
   267‚Üí

   269‚Üí                ForEach(1...5, id: \.self) { score in
   270‚Üí                    Button {
   271‚Üí                        value = score
   272‚Üí                    } label: {
   273‚Üí                        Text(\"\(score)\")
   274‚Üí                            .font(.subheadline)
   275‚Üí                            .fontWeight(.medium)
   276‚Üí                            .frame(maxWidth: .infinity)
   277‚Üí                            .padding(.vertical, 12)
   278‚Üí                            .background(value == score ? colorForValue(score) : Color(.secondarySystemBackground))
   279‚Üí                            .foregroundColor(value == score ? .white : .primary)
   280‚Üí                            .cornerRadius(8)
   281‚Üí                    }
   282‚Üí                    .buttonStyle(.plain)
   283‚Üí                }
   284‚Üí            }
   285‚Üí
   286‚Üí            HStack {
   287‚Üí                Text(minLabel)
   288‚Üí                    .font(.caption2)
   289‚Üí                    .foregroundColor(.secondary)
   290‚Üí                Spacer()
   291‚Üí                Text(maxLabel)
   292‚Üí                    .font(.caption2)
   293‚Üí                    .foregroundColor(.secondary)
   294‚Üí            }
   295‚Üí        }
   296‚Üí    }
   297‚Üí
   298‚Üí    private func colorForValue(_ value: Int) -> Color {
   299‚Üí        switch value {
   300‚Üí        case 1: return .green
   301‚Üí        case 2: return .mint
   302‚Üí        case 3: return .yellow
   303‚Üí        case 4: return .orange
   304‚Üí        case 5: return .red
   305‚Üí        default: return .gray
   306‚Üí        }
   307‚Üí    }
   308‚Üí}
   309‚Üí
   310‚Üístruct OptionalConditionScoreSelector: View {
   311‚Üí    let title: String
   312‚Üí    let description: String
   313‚Üí    @Binding var value: Int?
   314‚Üí    let minLabel: String
   315‚Üí    let maxLabel: String
   316‚Üí    var isInverted: Bool = false
   317‚Üí
   318‚Üí    var body: some View {
   319‚Üí        VStack(alignment: .leading, spacing: 8) {
   320‚Üí            HStack {
   321‚Üí                Text(title)
   322‚Üí                    .font(.subheadline)
   323‚Üí                    .fontWeight(.medium)
   324‚Üí                Text(\"(Optional)\")
   325‚Üí                    .font(.caption)
   326‚Üí                    .foregroundColor(.secondary)
   327‚Üí                Spacer()
   328‚Üí                if let v = value {
   329‚Üí                    Text(\"\(v)\")
   330‚Üí                        .font(.headline)
   331‚Üí                        .foregroundColor(colorForValue(v))
   332‚Üí                } else {
   333‚Üí                    Text(\"-\")
   334‚Üí                        .font(.headline)
   335‚Üí                        .foregroundColor(.secondary)
   336‚Üí                }
   337‚Üí            }
   338‚Üí
   339‚Üí            Text(description)
   340‚Üí                .font(.caption)
   341‚Üí                .foregroundColor(.secondary)
   342‚Üí
   343‚Üí            HStack(spacing: 8) {
   344‚Üí                ForEach(1...5, id: \.self) { score in
   345‚Üí                    Button {
   346‚Üí                        if value == score {
   347‚Üí                            value = nil
   348‚Üí                        } else {
   349‚Üí                            value = score
   350‚Üí                        }
   351‚Üí                    } label: {
   352‚Üí                        Text(\"\(score)\")
   353‚Üí                            .font(.subheadline)
   354‚Üí                            .fontWeight(.medium)
   355‚Üí                            .frame(maxWidth: .infinity)
   356‚Üí                            .padding(.vertical, 12)
   357‚Üí                            .background(value == score ? colorForValue(score) : Color(.secondarySystemBackground))
   358‚Üí                            .foregroundColor(value == score ? .white : .primary)
   359‚Üí                            .cornerRadius(8)
   360‚Üí                    }
   361‚Üí                    .buttonStyle(.plain)
   362‚Üí                }
   363‚Üí            }
   364‚Üí
   365‚Üí            HStack {
   366‚Üí                Text(minLabel)
   367‚Üí                    .font(.caption2)
   368‚Üí                    .foregroundColor(.secondary)
   369‚Üí                Spacer()
   370‚Üí                Text(maxLabel)
   371‚Üí                    .font(.caption2)
   372‚Üí                    .foregroundColor(.secondary)
   373‚Üí            }
   374‚Üí        }
   375‚Üí    }
   376‚Üí
   377‚Üí    private func colorForValue(_ value: Int) -> Color {
   378‚Üí        if isInverted {
   379‚Üí            switch value {
   380‚Üí            case 1: return .red
   381‚Üí            case 2: return .orange
   382‚Üí            case 3: return .yellow
   383‚Üí            case 4: return .mint
   384‚Üí            case 5: return .green
   385‚Üí            default: return .gray
   386‚Üí            }
   387‚Üí        } else {
   388‚Üí            switch value {
   389‚Üí            case 1: return .green
   390‚Üí            case 2: return .mint
   391‚Üí            case 3: return .yellow
   392‚Üí            case 4: return .orange
   393‚Üí            case 5: return .red
   394‚Üí            default: return .gray
   395‚Üí            }
   396‚Üí        }
   397‚Üí    }
   398‚Üí}
   399‚Üí
   400‚Üístruct ConditionRow: View {
   401‚Üí    let condition: MorningCondition
   402‚Üí
   403‚Üí    var body: some View {
   404‚Üí        HStack {
   405‚Üí            VStack(alignment: .leading, spacing: 4) {

   410‚Üí                    ConditionBadge(label: \"Done\", value: condition.owatteruFeeling)
   411‚Üí                    if let sleepiness = condition.daytimeSleepiness {

   427‚Üí
   428‚Üí    private var statusEmoji: String {
   429‚Üí        switch condition.overallScore {
   430‚Üí        case 0..<2: return \"üòä\"
   431‚Üí        case 2..<2.5: return \"üôÇ\"
   432‚Üí        case 2.5..<3.5: return \"üòê\"
   433‚Üí        case 3.5..<4.5: return \"üòî\"
   434‚Üí        default: return \"üòµ\"
   435‚Üí        }
   436‚Üí    }
   437‚Üí

   465‚Üí
   466‚Üí    private func colorForValue(_ value: Int) -> Color {
   467‚Üí        switch value {
   468‚Üí        case 1: return .green
   469‚Üí        case 2: return .mint
   470‚Üí        case 3: return .yellow
   471‚Üí        case 4: return .orange
   472‚Üí        case 5: return .red
